25a2(1): dang / ku na la las sotshogs pa bya'i khru mang po dus swa snyand cing 'jam la yid du 'ong ba rnam pa du ma 'byind pas ni/ bar snang la lha bzhin du so so'i nga ros rol mo'i skra dbyangs 'byin / lha'i rin po che sna tshogs kyi bdug spos kyi snod/ yangs shing che ba bye ba
25a3(1): khrag khrig brgya stong du ma thams cad kyang be dur+ya dang / an da rnyil dang / shel dang yug gi yu ba can dag gnod sbyin gyi bdag po gzugs bzang dang / dbang po'i tog dang / rang rod can dang / ba ku la dang / lngas chen dang / shag kyi 'phel las tshogs pa'
25a4(1): bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong du ma dag gi lag pa gnyis na gtun 'dzind pa bzhin du thogs te/ spos sbrul gyi snying po 'go shi re sha dang / sri na la dang / ha ri dang / ma la ya dang / tsan dan dmar po dang / a ga ru las sotshogs pas bkang ba'i du ba ni 'thul/ 
25a5(1): phyogs so so nas lhags pa'i rgyal po dbang che ba/ dbang che bar grags pa rnams rta dang / bal glang rgyand kyis shi nad tu brgyand cing ma zhon bar khrid pa'i tshogs du ma dang / shing rta dang dpung bu chung gis yongs su bskor cing 'phreng ba dang / lnga ldi mang po
25a6(1): rin po che'i 'phreng ba lag na thogs shing sngon logs nas rkang gos 'gro'o// rta dang glang po che legs par brgyand pa ma zhon par khrid pa dag kyang rang gi stabs kyis dngom par 'gro zhing skad yid du 'ong la snyand pa 'byind to// tshangs
25a7(1): pa yang bcom ldan 'das kyi g.yas phyogs nas mchod pa dang / rim 'gro bsnyen bkur byed cing 'gro'o// g.yon phyogs nas ni lha'i dbang po brgya byin lha'i bu dbang skye ba dbang che bar grags pa rgya che zhing rlabs che ba bgrang ba las 'das pa'
25a8(1): rnams lha'i cod pan bzang po dang / kadu bu rgyan can dang / rna tsa dang / gdu bu dang / me tog rna rgyan dang / rin po che'i cod tsong dang / me tog ki 'phreng bas lus brgya nad cing gzugs mngon par snang bas/ lha'i me tog man da ra dang / mdog mdzes
25a9(1): dang / ko bi de ra dang / sA la ka dang / ku ra ba ka dang / tsam pa ka dang / dong ka'i me tog dang / mya ngan 'tshang dang / skya sngar dang / a d+hi mu ka ta dang / ud pal dang / ba ku la dang / mal li ka dang / kun da dang / ke sa ra dang
25a10(1): ma dang / ku mu da dang / pad ma dkar po dang / dri mchog dang / rin po che pad ma'i 'phreng ba dang / rin po che'i a ga ru dang / shing rin po che'i 'bras bu can dag lag na thogs shing / sil snyan sna tshogs brgya tong ni shi na tu bkrol
25a11(1): gos bye ba ni g.yob cing a la la zhes ka zha'i sgra dag ni 'byin da/ me tog gi char chen po ni rab tu 'bebs shing / bcom ldan 'das mchod pa bya ba'i phyir/ nam mkha'i ngos thams cad bar mtshams myed par gang bar 'khod do// 
25b1(1): me tog dang spos dang 'phreng ba dang / byug pa dang / phye ma dang / rin po che'i char rab tu 'bebs shing / bcom ldan 'das chu dron yod pa'i sgo nas/ rgyal po'i khab kyi grong khyer chen por gdugs tshod la gshegs so// de'i chos nyid 'di yin
25b2(1): / de la 'di skad ces bya'o// sangs rgyas de bzhin gshegs pas dus pa khye nang nas/ dpam tho yon tan kund kyis rab brgya dang pa// zhing rnams bsam gyis kyi khyab sngar mdzad cing // bcom ldan gyi yi seng ge gshegs
25b3(1): par gyur pa// s+yan ras ke zigs dang mthul cen don yod dang // spos kyi bal rmang rin cen lag bzangs dang // rin cen tog dang 'brung pa dkal dpal go dpa // de dang gzhan dag rgyal ba'i zham 'bring byed// g.yas phyogs na ni myi
25b4(1): 'pham 'dug gyur da te// de mying byams pa yon tan mtha' yas phrug/ bar du mchod sangs rgyas 'gyur ba ste// bsod nams ye shes tshogs kyang rab tu rdzogs// byams dang btang snyoms dga' bas lus bsgoms shing // chos kyi bdag nyid
25b5(1): chen po snying rjes bskyed// yon tan mtha' yas thub dbang yon tan sems// bde gshegs thugs rje can gyi zham ring byed// de'i rjes la bskol pa bzang po'i// blo gros chen po ldan pa ci snyed pa'i// sangs rgyas hong du bzhis ma tshang ba dag/ de
25b6(1): ngag gis kyang byams pa mdun tu bad rang // gang sngon rgyal po'i khab kyi grong khyer 'dir// bskal pa dag la rgyal ba mtha' yas mchod// tha ba mdzes pa'i 'od la dra lnga'i lus// zla 'od dpa' bo yang ni mdun na 'dug/ snying rje mchog gi g.yor phyos
25b7(1): 'dug pa ni// 'jam dpal bye ba brgya phrag mang po dang / dpa' bo rdzu 'phrul stobs kyis mngon 'phags pa// brgya phrag mtha' yas zhing du 'gro ba'o// de'i 'og tu nyan thos dge 'dun te// sha ri li bu 'og ye bu dgal nag po dang // 'od srung rab 'byor de dga'
25b8(1): bo ka pi na// bzang ldan rgyal po de bzhin ko'u di ts+yai// kun dka' de bzhin gnas brtan sgra kacan zin// legs 'ongs kron ci kang po 'char ba po// nam ku gsung cen nyer 'khor ma 'gags pa// ral pa can ni tong du chang ba dag/ nyan thos dge 'dun
25b9(1): sa rnams pa kyang / da' du rnams cin nas kyang cig she/ dab pa 'ang dang par 'dags rgyas pas// drang thongasas papas byo 'dud pa byed// ma med dang mamam yi rnams kyis/ sangs rgyapa chis tan ston pa mangs
25b10(1): bdar da te// thugs rjer ldan pa'i myi'i seng ge gshegs// sems can stong rnams rab tu tha rad par mdzad// nyon zla tha chungs zla ba nya ba ltar// skar tshogs dbang po yongs su dag pa bzhin// tshangs pa stong phrag dag ni brgya mang gis
25b11(1): mtshungs pa myed pa'i nyon pa yongs su bsor // grong khyer gyi ni sgo nying zhabs bzhag ste/ nags chal stug por bcas pa'i sa yang g.yos// swa dang lA myin lto 'bya'i tshogs rnams kyang // me tog bzang po dri mchog 'thor bar byed// 
27a1(1): byed// rgyal ba grong gshegs sangs rgyas rnam mdzes pa// de tshe 'od rnams thams cad yod myi mngon// tshogs can dang ni bder gshegs lam bzhud de// gang tu stobs bcu yi ni zhabs 'jog par// sa la
27a2(1): pad ma dag ni stong phrag brgya// mdab ma bye ba sor ldan gtsang ma zung // 'drend pa grong khyer mchog tu gshegs pa'i tshe// de la nyal nyil myi gtsang myed par gyur // grong khyer thams cad dri mchog gdug pa yi// spos dad yid du 'ong
27a3(1): ba kun nas ldang // grong dang srang rnams yongs su dag gyur da te// rdo dang gseg ma myed cing spos chus btab// stobs bcu ldan pa'i bsod nams de 'dra ste// rnam pa sna tshogs me tog sil ma bkram// gnod sbyin brgya hong gtum por
27a4(1): sems pa dag/ sangs rgyas myi dbang gser 'dra mthong bas ni// 'dren la dga' ba rgya che rab bskyed nas// sangs rgyas chos dang dge 'dun skyabs su 'gro// lha rnams bye ba dang ni brgya phrag stong // myi dbang lta bar 'ongs pa de dag kun// bde bar
27a5(1): gas la me tog char phab he// me tog gtor da nas nam mkha'i dkyil na 'dug/ rgyal la myi yis me tog gang gtor da pa// nam mkha'i ngos la me tog gdugs su gyur da// lnga rnams kyis ni me tog gtor da pa yang // sa heng lha'i me tog bkram
27a6(1): bar gyur nga/ lha dang myi dang grul bum srin po rnams/ de mthong nas ni nam yang ngoms myi myong / mgon po stobs bcu ldan pa mthong nas kyang / rab tu da ga' zhing sems bde rangs par gyur da/ nas che skyes bu mchog gi sru mthong nas
27a7(1): sems can thams cad dga' mgu rangs gyurd pas// lnga'i me tog la yang yid myi sems// de dag la ni ngo mtsha rang 'dzind pa myed// stobs bcu'i g.yas phyogs na ni tshangs pa ste// de bzhin g.yon na brgya byin lha'i rgyal// nam mkha'i dkyil
27a8(1): na lha mangs bye 'khod de/ skyes bu mchog la shi nad tu gus pa skyed// lha dang lha sbyin dag gis rgyal ba bskord// lha dang myi'i dpal gzi kun phrogs nas// zhabs mthil sa la ri mo 'byin bzhin du// grong khyer du ni bcom ldan spyan drangs
27a9(1): gshegs// sku lus dpe' byad bzang pos rgyas pa ni// nam mkha' skar ma dag gis gang ba bzhin// nam mkha' le ni zla ba nya ba ltar// rgyal po'i khab na sangs rgyas las me bzhugs// nor bu rin cen rnam dag bzang po ni// nyes pa'i
27a10(1): spyod bral rab tu snang bar byed// phyogs dang phyogs mtshams su yang 'od gcang 'thung // de bzhin rgyal ba 'jig rten dkun sdang mdzad// lha dang lnga byin dag gis rgyal ba bskor// mya'i gtso bo rgyal po'i khab du gshegs// 'bam
27a11(1): mthil sa la ri mo 'byin bzhin du// zla 'od gzho nu'i khyim du sangs rgyas gshegs// grong khyer mchog ni kund tu legs brgya nad te// rgyal mtshan bye ba phrag hong rab tu bsgreb// de'i sa kun spos bzang rnam par thugs// yid 'ong
27b1(1): de bzhin dbyar da kyi me tog gtor da// gang che ba der gshegs gtam rnams nyond pa na// mgon po srang bzhud myi la thugs brtse'i phyir// rgyal bas der ni 'phrul ba rnam skul te// de dag la yang sangs rgyas chos bzang ston / 
27b2(1): srog chags brgya stong dag gis de thos nas// sangs rgyas ye shes mchog la smon lam 'debs// nam bdag 'di 'dra'i ye shes thob snyam ste// bsam pa mkhyen nas rgyal ba lung yang ston // gang gis rgyal ba myi dbang s+yan 'dras pa'i// 
27b3(1): sbyin pa de ni mu mtha' myed gyur da te// rnyed mchog bsam gyis myi khyab des rnyed ces// la la dag ni de la mos pa skyed// 'khor ba dag na shi nad tu mthong dka' ba// skyed dgu dag la phan mdzad thugs kyang brtse// thugs rje can de bdag gis sang
27b4(1): la yang // s+yan drang snyam du la la sems kyang skyed// la la ba gas mchog gi steng 'dug cing // lus ni shi nad tu sdug cing mdzes par brgyad// byang chub sems mchog dam pa bskyed nas ni// stobs bcu ldan la lha'i me tog 'phor// la las
27b5(1): pra myed sems mchog rab bskyed nas// me tog tsam pa mdzes pa'i 'phreng ba dang // a ti mug ta de bzhin dbyar da kyi spos// dar gyi lda ldi dag kyang la la 'thor// kha cig gos kyis shi nad tu lus brgyand te// me tog bzang po dag kyang thogs
27b6(1): shing 'greng // me tog sna tshogs dar gyi lnga ldi thogs// rgyal ba mthu' cen de'i phyogaHsa su 'thor// la la pad ma dang ni ku mu da// ud pa la gser gyi me to ga bzang po 'thor// la la rin cen me tog de 'thor te// la la tsan dan phye ma 'thor
27b7(1): bar byed// 'drend pa grong khyer mchog tu gshegs pa'i tshe// ngo mtsha dadang dpag tu myed pa rnams kyang 'byung // mtshungs myed de dag brjod par myi nus te// sangs rgyas ye shes skye bo bye yangs bkod// mye che myi gdung bden pa mthong ba dang / 
27b8(1): gzhan yang gya nom sdang dang shin tu mthong // de bzhin 'og sbyin 'dod chags bral ba rnams// thams cad myi dbang lta phyir nye bar lhags// de bzhin dge ba'i lha rnams dpag myed dang // dge chub lha gzhan dag kyang sems dka' zhing / 
27b9(1): dge rgyas khrag khrig dpag tu myed pa rnams// 'drend pa drang srong chen po lta phyir lhags// tshad myed 'od kyang de bzhin dpag myed dang // 'od chung gi ni lha rnams ci yod dang // 'od gsal ba yang khrag khrig mang po der// 'jig rten da mgon po

27b11(1): mas dang // gzhan yang 'phrul dka'i sems can dag pa dang // dga' ldan 'thab bral lha rnams rab dga' zhing // thams cad sangs rgyas phyag 'tshal nye bar lhags// brgya byin lnga rgyal sum bcu rtsa gsum pa// lha'i bu mo bye ba brgya
28a1(1): drang skags// 'di dran pa rtog ca ya pa rab 'bebs zhing // sangs rgyas thub dbangs phyir nye bam sngags// phyogs bzhil 'jig rten du pyor ba can po yang // rnam thos su dang klu dbang myig myi bza // yul 'khor
28a2(1): srung dang 'phags skyes sems dga' ste// de kun myi dbang nyod cing nye bar lhags// gnod sbyin rgyal po mthul ldan ir bir yang // dga' ba skyes shing gnod sbyin brgyas bskor da te// nam mkha'i dkyil na 'dug cing sems dka'
28a3(1): nas// me tog sna tshogs du ma'i char yang 'bebs// rtag tu myos dang 'phreng 'dzin da lha rnams kyang // spos dang 'phreng ba rnam pa sna tshogs thogs// 'khor dang bcas pa thams cad sems dga' ying // de ni skyes bu mchog la mchod pa
28a4(1): da// gnod sbyin lag na gzhong thogs mang po yang // gnod sbyin bu mo de dag rab brgya na te// gnod sbyin rol mo rab tu snyand pa dang // shi nad tu yid 'ong brgyas ni sangs rgyas mchod// gru dbyangs sil snyan du 'jam zhing snyan du

28a8(1): ni pad ma che// de bzhin nor yod mtha' yas gdengs ka can// de dag khyu mchog drung du nyer lpags te// bde bar gshegs la gus par rab tu 'dud// klu'i rgyal po nor bu yid dga' zhing // khru mchog zhabs kyi drung du nye bar 'ongs// klu'i me tog

28b1(1): pa la yang mthon par 'thor// de bzhin klu'i rgyal po dus can yang // de bzhin gshegs pa'i drung du nyer 'ongs te// dga' zhing rin cen 'phreng ba mdzes mchog thogs// skyes bu dam pa la yang mchod rab byas// de nas bde gshegs
28b2(1): yon tan rjes dran zhing // gus pa chen po shind tu bskyed nas ni// gnyen mdab klu mang dag gis de bskord cing // 'drend pa'i bsngags pa rnam pa mang po rjod// de bzhin klu dbang dga' bo nye dga' dang // de bzhin 'jog po 'ge'u
28b3(1): tam nag po yang // rgyal ba lta zhing der ni nye bar 'ongs// bde bar gshegs pa'i zhabs la 'dud pa byed// klu'i rgyal po e la'i mdab ma yang // thub mchog rgyal ba'i 'od srung dran pa dang // bdag nyid myi khom skyes pa mthong nas ni//

28b5(1): pa skye bo'i lus 'di dang // klu'i skye gnas bdag gis rab spangs la// chos gang byang chub snying por skyes mchog gis// rtogs pa bsil ba bdag gis rtogs par bya// klu'i rgyal po rgya mtshol 'khor los spur// bye ba gsum snyed klu'i 'khor
28b6(1): skor da// chu lha gzi can rin cen do shal thogs// bcom ldan 'das la ma chod phyir nye bar 'ongs// rgyal ba la ni rdo 'phangs des bzung ste// de tshe nam mkha' yang 'dug gyur da pa// rgyal po'i khab kyi gnod sbyin ci zhig 'dzin da//

28b8(1): rna dang ni khab su dang // gnod sbyin 'brog gnas 'jigs byed de bzhin te// gang gnas ring 'dug gnod sbyin bong bu dag/ rgyal ba rang thung drung du nye bar lhags// dbang po'i tog dang gzugs bzang rang rod can// ba ku la dang rnam 'phel

29a1(1): grog ma khar drang srong mchog/ dka' bar gnas dang myi'u thung spend pa rnams// 'drend pa lta zhing grong khyer mchog tu lhags// drang srong mthong nas de tshe drang srong dgal// thub rgyal zhabs mchog la ni phyag 'tshald cing
29a2(1): 'jig rtend sgrol la phyag byas mngon bstod de// thal mo sbyar nas dpa' bo'i spyan sngar 'greng // 'jig rten da ci yod drang srong mang po kun// de dag myi dbang lta bar nyer lpags te// mthong nas mchod pa rgya cher byas nas kyang /

29a4(1): 'khod// grong brgya dang ni 'dzam grong nags tshal na// gnas shing rten pa'i lha rnams gang yod dang // grong gi lha mo ma lus thams cad kyang // nye bar lhags shing gtso bo mchod pa byed// nags tshal gyi yang lha rnams mtha' yas
29a5(1): dang // ri'i lha rnams thams cad nye bar 'ongs// 'beb chu'i lha kun mtha' dag de bzhin du// 'drend pa mchod pa byed cing nye bar lhags// mya ngam dgon pa'i lha mo brgya rnams dang // ri me'i lha mo co snyed pa lus dang // mtsho dang
29a6(1): chu myig rdzing gi lha rnams dang // rgya mtsho'i lha yang sangs rgyas drung du lhags// lha dang lha myin klu dang gnod sbyin tshogs// myi 'am ci dang grul bum na ma mkhal lding // de bzhin yi dgas srul po mang po dag/ skyes bu mchog
29a7(1): la ri mor bya ba byed// 'dre nad pa grong khyer mchog der gshegs pa na// rgyal ba mchog la de dag mchod pa byed// lha dang lha myin klu dang gnod sbyin rgyal// lta bas rtag tu chog par yod myi 'gyur// sngon gyi srid par 'jig rtend mgon po yis// 
29a8(1): sngon gyi rgyal ba dag la mchod mchog byas/ bsod nams 'bras bu sbyind pa de 'dra ste// skyes bu myi dbang lta bas ngoms myi myong // rgyal bas sangs rgyas zhing du 'od btang tshe// lhun po de bzhin rab lhun 'khor yug ri// kha ba can gyi ro dang
29a9(1): spos ngad ldang // de dag rgyal ba'i 'od la sgrib pa myed// sangs rgyas zhing 'di rgya mtshol ci yod pa// de dag de tshe sa dang 'dra bar gyur pa// sangs rgyas zhing 'di thams cad kund tu yang // me tog dag gis gtor da cing mnyam par gyur pa// 'od

30a1(1): / nas// mya ngan 'das pa mchog tu mchi// myi mnyam mnyam pa'i mgon gcig pa la de skad bstod// gzhonu yid kyang rab tu dkar gyur da tshig spras pa// sangs rgyas mtshungs myed bsam yas

33a6(1): rig/ de bzhin kund tu blo yang gtong // chos kun de'i rang bzhin te// rnam par dag pa nam mkha' bzhin// yid la rnams kyang 'byung ba myed// chos rnams thams cad shes pas na// khams gsum las ni rnam par grol// de la smon
33a7(1): lam 'debs pa myed// yang dag ci bzhin du ni mthor gyurd cing // ma log tshig sma rnam pa gzhan gyi spa// de'i tshig dang brjod pa thams cad kyang // rgyal ba dag gi mthu yis 'thung bar 'gyur// 'dod pa'i sa dang nyon mongs sa rnams dang / 
33a8(1): gzugs dang gzugs myed las kyang shi nad tu 'da'// chos rnams la ni yid kyang ma chags shing / rab tu dga' bas 'gro la phan par spyad// mying ki sa las 'das shing sA yang shes// ngo bo nyid kyis gsog tu gyurd pa ste// ci srid tsam
33a9(1): du yun ring brjod na yang // de la gnas par byed pa yod ma yin// 'dushe sa rab tu rtsub byed// lta ba log pa kur ram pa sa yang// tho yang ga ring du gtan la bab// btad pa nam mala' 'dra bar gyod// kal te 'dud bye bag khrig rnams/ 
33a10(1): rdo'i se pas dkrug phyir 'ongs kyang // bdud nams thams cad zi ya ma dand te// de'i dbang du 'gro phyi 'gyur// bdud kyi rgya bo rnam spangs te// dul khrims yongs dag gdung ba byed/ bsapa gtan dag gi 'des mas// 'jig
33a11(1): rten du song bar rab tu zhes// 'jig rten phung por smras pa yang // de dag stong par rab tu rig/ skye ba sred cing 'gag byed pas// chos rnams thams cad nas lakhal bzhin/ de dag bdag nyid gtong byed kyi// stobs la
33b1(1): bcu'i tshul khrims thas kyi gtong // den tshul khrims pa rol phyinang // gar spo dad par yang skye bar 'gyur // sangs rgyas zhi dunas pa'agro// sangs rgyas zhag zhig pa sa mnatha// man 'am dag ni myi 'dod de// sdom lam rnam
33b2(1): ni yongs myi gtong // chos nyid dag ni de s+yod che// skad cig brtson 'grus nyams myi byed// phyogs bcu'i ni sangs rgyas kyis// de ni shin tu btod pa yod// de khyer gno nu ting 'dzidad las// chom 'di dag ni rab thos nas// shes
33b3(1): kyi khe ni rnam spongs la// skye bo mang la chos rab ston // sangs rgyas yon tan yang ldan pa// rang 'thung 'gyur ba gang 'dod pas// dge ba 'di la rab bslabs na// stobs bcu 'chang ba sangs rgyas 'gyur//

33b5(1): chen po tha na myed pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar 'dod pas/ ting nge 'dzin dnges par banyan dal pa la mkhas par bya'o// gzho nu de la ting nge 'dzin nges par bstand pa gang zhe na/ gang chos thams cad kyi ci
33b6(1): lta ba bzhin nyid dang / mnyam pa nyid myinyas pa myed pa dang / myi rtog pa rnam par myi rtog pa/ rnam par ma bsgrubs pa kun nas slong ba myed pa/ skye ba myed pa/ 'gog pa myed pa/ rtog pa dang rnam par rtog pa dang / kun rtog pa yongs su chad
33b7(1): sems kyi dmyigs pa myed pa/ yid la byed pa myed pa/ rnam par rig pa yongs su chad pa/ 'dod chags dang zhe sdangar dang gti mug yongs su chad pa/ mtha' myed pa/ mthar yid la byed pa dang bral ba/ yid la byed pa yongs su chad pa/ phung po dang
33b8(1): khams dang skye mched kyi ngo bo nyid shes pa/ dran pa dang blo gros dang rtogs pa dang / khrel yod pa dang / brtan pa dang cho ga dang spyod yul dang / nan tan gyi gnas su gyur da pa/ nyon mongs pa myed pa'i sa zhi ba'i sa/ smos pa thams cad yongs su chad pa'i
33b9(1): nga chub sems dpa'/ thams cad kyi bslab pa de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi spyod yul/ yon tan thams cad yongs su rdzogs pa 'di ni gzho nu ting nge 'dzind nges par bstand pa zhes bya ste/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po ting
33b10(1): nge 'dzin nges par bstand pa 'di la gnas pa ni ting nge 'dzin dang ma bral ba yin/ sems 'khrul pa myed pa yin/ snying rje chen po dang ldan zhing sems can dpag tu myed pa'i don byed pa yin no// de nas de'i tshe bcom ldan 'das kyis tshigs
33b11(1): su bcad pa 'di dag gsungs so// ting 'dzin pa mnyam pa byed pa yis// shinang tu mthong dka' phra zhing 'i// 'du shes thams cad bcom pa ste// de phyir ti po 'dzind ces bya// rtog pa myed cing rnam rtog byed// gzung ba myed cing bstanang
36a1(1): 'khod pa rnams// bcom ldan 'das kyis don ldan gsung thos nas// thams cad 'drin la rab tu dga' ba skyed// tshig ni rab tu stand cing bza la 'thad// mnyen zhing 'jam la yid 'ong dus dang 'byor da// gsung gi yan
36a2(1): lag dpag tu myed dang ldan// phar byed skye bo mang po thar byed pa// sil snyan brgya song dpag tu myed pa dang // lha'i dbyangs sba dga' bar 'gyur ba'i mchog/ shi dad tu snyand pa dus gcig 'byor da gyur da kyang // bder gshegs gsung gcig gis
36a3(1): lad kyis non// khu byug bya mang 'jam pa'i sgra 'byind dang // kun la shi nad tu yid 'thad dbyangs snyan dang// bya tshogs mang po thams cad sgra 'byind pa// sangs rgyas gsung gi char yang des myi phod// lha'i bu mo skra dbyangs snyan da pa dang // 
36a4(1): sil snyan da rol mo klu dbyangs 'jam pa dang // bi bang rdza rnga rnga cen dung gi sma// de dag sangs rgyas gsung gi char myi phod// khu brug ne tso re skegs sA rnams dang // zhur khrung rma bya myi 'am ci'i ske// swa dbyangs yid 'ong snyand pa ci yod pa
36a5(1): de dag sangs rgyas gsung gi char myi phod// snyand cing mnyen la yid 'ong dga' ba dang // shin tu mnyen la rab bsngags zhi ba'i tshig/ dbyangs rnams thams cad dus gcig bsgrag pa bas// de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsung mchog dgar
36a6(1): 'gyur yin// lha myi myi dbang lha ma yin rnams dang // srid gsum sems can mtha' dag ci yod pa// 'od byed rnams kyi 'od snang de dag ni// bder gsheg/ sa 'od gzer gcig gis zil kyis non// bder gshegs sku ni me tog rgyas
36a7(1): pa bzhin// mtshan rnams kun kyis sna tshogs sbas shing brgyand// bsod nams brgyas grub dag cing rnam par dang // rgyal ba'i su ni 'jig rten da kund tu ldan// dung ki sgra dang khar rnga s+pha snyan dang // rnga'i sgra dang de bzhin kim pa la'i
36a8(1): sgra// rab tu 'jam zhing 'thad pa'i swa de kun// sangs rgyas dbyangs kyi brgya'i char myi phod// sil snyan bye ba khrag khrig hong gi swa// sma skad gsang zhing mnyen pa lha'i 'dra// lha dang lha mo'i sgra dbyangs dkar 'gyur ba// sangs la
36a9(1): rgyas dbyangs kyi brgya'i char gyi phod// khrung zhung la bya dur pa khu byug dang // ngang pa kun la rnam yang bya'i tshogs// de dag sangs rgyas sgra snyan dus gcig tshogs pas kyang // sangs rgyas dbyangs kyi brgya'i char gyi phod// klu dang gnod
36a10(1): phyo la myin lto bye nga // sna dbang tshangs pa lnga'i bdag po'i sku// srid gsum yid 'ong 'ayad pa rtsa yod pa// de dag sangs rgyas dbyangs kyi cher gyi phod// tshangs pa'i 'od dang lha'i dbang po dang // nyi pa dang ror bu rin cer 'od
36a11(1): srin kyi 'dzi rnam pa sum dag/ kun kyang rgyal ma mo dkyis yis kyim nor// lus dang ngag dang yid kya ga nga tun pa yang dag/ ye she pa dag pa sring pa gsum dgos pa byed// phyi dbang yon tad dbyig tshogs yon tan mi
36b1(1): chen mngal// rang thub yon tan thams cad kyis ni mnyam myed mnyam// de snar stobs bcu bden pa gsung la 'dod nas ni// gan du yid kyang rab tu dka' bas tshig sbas pa// sangs rgyas gnal byed dpag yas la na mchod pa
36b2(1): las// sa pa zu pazhin 'das kyang sangs rgyas par nga sa smra// bde bar gshegs pa pa ris byed pa mchog ma khyen nas// phyi rab bags myed yi shes yanga' ba 'phrul ba pa dang // gcos 'an mas kyi mu 'o rnams pas dezhus te// 
36b3(1): 'drend pas gang gi slad du 'di ltar 'dzum pa mdzad// sa 'di dag kyang rnam pa drug du yongs su g.yos// lha dang klu rnams mkha' la 'dug cing rab dga' ste// shi nad tu sems rangs mgu bas sangs rgyas lta zhing mchis// bder
36b4(1): gshegs zi lad kyis ma non de dag lung bahand gsol// skyes bu mchog gi ye shes gang la zhugs pa si// bcom ldan 'das kyi nyan thos dag gi sa ma lags// rgyal ba khyod kyis gang gi slad du 'dzum mdzad pa// ye shes rnam
36b5(1): dag dpe' myed ye shes ma lus gsungs// shag kya'i seng ge stobs bcu mnga' zhing rnam 'drend pa// rkang gnyis gtso bo ye shes kyi yang pha rol du phyind// 'dod chags dang ni zhe sdang tha ba gti muka sel da// rab tu 'od snang mdzad pa khyod la
36b6(1): zhu ba lags// byang chub dam pa mchog 'dir rab tu tshol ba'i phyir// 'drend pa bskaldad pa gang 'ga'i bye snyed dang // de las lhag par yang ni pyad pa rab tu supyad// gang gi don tu 'dzum pa 'di mdzad bahand tu gsol// ye shes dam pa
36b7(1): mchog 'di rab tu tshol ba'i phyir// ton pas zhabs dang phyag kyang yongs su btang ba mdzad// sras dang btsun mo gnyen bshes ma lag phangs pa btang // thub pa 'jul ba bstand pa 'di'i rmugag lags// rta dang bal grang dang ni shi
36b8(1): kab tang dang // bran dang nor bu dngul dang mu tig khyod kyis btang // pyod pa mchog dpyod che ni khyod kyis ma btang ba// rin po che dang nor rdzas dag ni gang yang skyed// srid pa gsum na ye shes dag ni mchog tu gyur du// sems can thams
36b9(1): da kyini myod pa rab tu bakhyend// sems can khams dpathos pa dag la 'ang ya' sa shing rig// gang gi don tu 'dus pa 'di dag bstan pa ma dzang// rgya chegatso bo la ni gang gis mchod// gang ka dan ni rgya che yangs par 'gyur// kyang
36b10(1): yang bu sa rab tu mdzid// lus pa gang gi 'ong tu 'dus 'a sa dang // sa yang nas pa drug du rab gyig / das bye ba me nga sa kyi ba mdza// gsam gyi pa ma shi nga tu 'dagasas so// mjam na ya du na/ 
36b11(1): ma gyimatshu sems da su 'bru'i rim mang// tshul ba srin pa thams mi y-i chos skam sang mang ba sarna sa te// 'dren pa man ra 'i mangs su// rang rung dpa' ma byer dang / 
37a1(1): snyan bye ba khrag khrig bdungs pa'i// de dag sA ni nam mkha' 'di las gda'// bde bar gshegs pa'i dbyangs ni bsam gyi khyab// zhung zhung dang pa ka ma thing ka dang // zhu thug rgya tshogs mang po 'dus pa'i// sna dbyangs
37a2(1): rab tu snyand pa byung ba yang // de dag sangs rgyas dbyangs kyi char phyi phod// gang gis sbyin dang dul dang legs sdom rnams// sngon gyi bskal da pa mang por bsnyen pa bgyis// gang gis phyi'i gtso bo rab mchod na// su'i slad du 'jum pa 'a

37a4(1): da ltar thung dang ma byung ba der gshegs dang // myo rig tso bo thams cad rab tu mkhyen // de phyir skye dgu'i don tu zhu ba lags// srog chags kun kyi khyod yul mtha' yas dang // myi rnams gang gi bsam bci 'dra dang // skye dgu'i sos kyi
37a5(1): rgud kyang rab tu mkhyen // de phyir myi'i gcol zhu ba lags// rgyu dang rigs pa 'dul la mkhas pa dag/ sangs rgyas ye shes ci ltar thob snyam pa// spyod pa mchog la su dag pyod pa rnams// de phyir bdag ni rkang gnyis gtso la zhu//

37a8(1): yul dag gi pha rol da byind// de phyir mgon po la ni bdag zhu'o// tshul khrims ye shes yon tan pha rol phyind// dus gsum la ma ye shes mtshungs byed 'jug/ khyod la 'khrul da pa dag ni khyi yang las// su'i srad du 'dul ba 'di dag bstan/

38b5(1): spobs dang ldan par gyur pa// kun tu rtag par tshangs par spyod pa s+yad// de ni phyi dus 'jigs pa chen po la// 'di la ma pham khyod nyid nga'i dbang // rtag tu tshangs spyod gtsang la gnas nas ni// ting nge 'dzin 'di shi nad tu rgyas byed/
